"""

from django.contrib import admin
from .models import (
    FeastRepository, DataSource, Entity, 
    AuditLog, LLMChatSession, LLMMessage
)


@admin.register(FeastRepository)
class FeastRepositoryAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['name', 'location', 'default_owner', 'get_node_count', 'updated_at', 'created_by']
    list_filter = ['created_at', 'updated_at', 'default_owner']
    search_fields = ['name', 'description']
    readonly_fields = ['created_at', 'updated_at', 'json_hash', 'last_synced_at']
    
    fieldsets = (
        ('Basic Info', {
            'fields': ('name', 'location', 'description', 'default_owner')
        }),
        ('Architecture Data', {
            'fields': ('architecture_json', 'settings', 'json_hash'),
            'classes': ('collapse',)
        }),
        ('Sync Info', {
            'fields': ('last_synced_at',),
            'classes': ('collapse',)
        }),
        ('Metadata', {
            'fields': ('created_by', 'created_at', 'updated_at'),
            'classes': ('collapse',)
        }),
    )

    def get_node_count(self, obj):
        return obj.get_node_count()
    get_node_count.short_description = 'Nodes'


@admin.register(DataSource)
class DataSourceAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['name', 'repository', 'kind', 'category', 'debezium_supported', 'owned_by', 'feast_connection_type']
    list_filter = ['kind', 'feast_connection_type', 'created_at', 'repository']
    search_fields = ['name', 'description', 'connection_string']
    readonly_fields = ['debezium_supported', 'category', 'created_at', 'updated_at']
    
    fieldsets = (
        ('Basic Info', {
            'fields': ('repository', 'name', 'kind', 'description', 'tags')
        }),
        ('Ownership & Access', {
            'fields': ('owned_by', 'access_process'),
            'classes': ('collapse',)
        }),
        ('Connection', {
            'fields': ('connection_string', 'topic', 'feast_connection_type'),
            'classes': ('collapse',)
        }),
        ('Security', {
            'fields': ('column_security',),
            'classes': ('collapse',)
        }),
        ('Position', {
            'fields': ('pos_x', 'pos_y'),
            'classes': ('collapse',)
        }),
        ('Computed', {
            'fields': ('debezium_supported', 'category', 'created_at', 'updated_at'),
            'classes': ('collapse',)
        }),
    )


@admin.register(Entity)
class EntityAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['name', 'repository', 'join_key', 'updated_at']
    list_filter = ['created_at', 'repository']
    search_fields = ['name', 'description']
    readonly_fields = ['created_at', 'updated_at']


@admin.register(AuditLog)
class AuditLogAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['timestamp', 'user', 'action', 'resource_type', 'resource_name']
    list_filter = ['action', 'resource_type', 'timestamp']
    search_fields = ['resource_name', 'details']
    readonly_fields = ['timestamp']
    date_hierarchy = 'timestamp'

    fields = ['role', 'content', 'query_type', 'total_tokens', 'created_at']
    can_delete = False
    max_num = 10  # Show last 10 messages

"""
Simplified Groq LLM Client for Feast Architect
"""
import os
import json
from typing import Dict, Optional
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict

# Load environment variables from .env file if python-dotenv is available
try:
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
    load_dotenv()  # Loads variables from .env file into environment
    DOTENV_AVAILABLE = True
except ImportError:
    DOTENV_AVAILABLE = False

try:
    from groq import Groq
    GROQ_AVAILABLE = True
except ImportError:
    GROQ_AVAILABLE = False


@dataclass
class LLMContext:
    """Context about the repository for LLM queries."""
    repo_name: str = "Unknown"
    node_count: int = 0
    edge_count: int = 0
    data_sources: int = 0
    entities: int = 0
    feature_views: int = 0
    services: int = 0
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return asdict(self)


class GroqLLMClient:
    """Simple Groq API client."""
    
    DEFAULT_MODEL = "llama-3.3-70b-versatile"
    
    SYSTEM_PROMPTS = {
        "default": "You are a Feast feature store expert. Provide concise, actionable advice.",
        "generate_code": "You are a Feast code generation expert. Output valid Python code.",
        "optimize": "You are a Feast performance expert. Focus on TTL, materialization, and serving.",
        "lineage": "You are a data lineage expert. Trace data flow from source to service.",
        "validate": "You are a Feast validator. Check for errors and anti-patterns."
    }
    
    def __init__(self, api_key: Optional[str] = None):
        if not GROQ_AVAILABLE:
            raise RuntimeError("Install groq: pip install groq")
        
        # Priority: 1) passed argument, 2) environment variable, 3) raise error
        self.api_key = api_key or os.environ.get("GROQ_API_KEY")
        if not self.api_key:
            raise RuntimeError(
                "GROQ_API_KEY not found. Set it in your .env file or environment. "
                "Create a .env file with: GROQ_API_KEY=your_api_key_here"
            )
        
        self.client = Groq(api_key=self.api_key)
    
    def query(
        self,
        message: str,
        context: Optional[LLMContext] = None,
        query_type: str = "default",
        stream: bool = False
    ) -> Dict:
        """Send query to Groq API."""
        
        # Build system prompt
        system = self.SYSTEM_PROMPTS.get(query_type, self.SYSTEM_PROMPTS["default"])
        if context:
            system += f"\n\nRepository: {context.repo_name} ({context.node_count} nodes, {context.edge_count} edges)"
        
        messages = [
            {"role": "system", "content": system},
            {"role": "user", "content": message}
        ]
        
        completion = self.client.chat.completions.create(
            model=self.DEFAULT_MODEL,
            messages=messages,
            temperature=0.7,
            max_completion_tokens=2048,
            stream=stream
        )
        
        if stream:
            return completion  # Generator
        
        return {
            "response": completion.choices[0].message.content,
            "model": self.DEFAULT_MODEL,
            "usage": {
                "prompt_tokens": completion.usage.prompt_tokens if completion.usage else 0,
... (truncated)

"""
Feast Architect - Simplified Django Models
"""
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User
from django.core.serializers.json import DjangoJSONEncoder
import json


class FeastRepository(models.Model):
    """Main repository container for Feast architecture."""
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255, unique=True)
    location = models.CharField(max_length=500, default='/opt/feast/feature_repo')
    description = models.TextField(blank=True)
    default_owner = models.CharField(max_length=255, default='Data Platform Team')
    
    # Complete architecture stored as JSON (nodes, edges, canvas state)
    architecture_json = models.JSONField(
        default=dict,
        help_text="Complete diagram state including nodes, edges, positions",
        encoder=DjangoJSONEncoder
    )
    
    # Repository settings
    settings = models.JSONField(default=dict, encoder=DjangoJSONEncoder)
    
    # Sync tracking
    last_synced_at = models.DateTimeField(null=True, blank=True)
    json_hash = models.CharField(max_length=64, blank=True, help_text="MD5 hash of last saved JSON")
    
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
    updated_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now=True)
    created_by = models.ForeignKey(
        User, 
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL, 
        null=True, 
        related_name='repositories'
    )

    class Meta:
        ordering = ['-updated_at']

    def __str__(self):
        return self.name

    def get_node_count(self):
        """Count nodes from stored JSON."""
        nodes = self.architecture_json.get('nodes', {})
        return len(nodes) if isinstance(nodes, dict) else len(nodes)

    def get_edge_count(self):
        """Count edges from stored JSON."""
        return len(self.architecture_json.get('edges', []))


class DataSource(models.Model):
    """Data source with ownership and access tracking."""
    
    DATABASE_TYPES = [
        # Relational
        ('postgres', 'PostgreSQL'),
        ('mysql', 'MySQL'),
        ('sqlserver', 'SQL Server'),
        ('oracle', 'Oracle'),
        ('sqlite', 'SQLite'),
        # NoSQL
        ('mongodb', 'MongoDB'),
        ('dynamodb', 'DynamoDB'),
        ('cassandra', 'Cassandra'),
        ('couchbase', 'Couchbase'),
        ('elasticsearch', 'Elasticsearch'),
        # Cloud Warehouses
        ('snowflake', 'Snowflake'),
        ('bigquery', 'BigQuery'),
        ('redshift', 'Redshift'),
        ('databricks', 'Databricks Delta Lake'),
        ('synapse', 'Azure Synapse'),
        # Streaming
        ('kafka', 'Apache Kafka'),
        ('kinesis', 'AWS Kinesis'),
        ('pulsar', 'Apache Pulsar'),
        ('eventhubs', 'Azure Event Hubs'),
        # Object Storage
        ('s3', 'Amazon S3 (Parquet)'),
        ('gcs', 'Google Cloud Storage'),
        ('azureblob', 'Azure Blob Storage'),
        ('minio', 'MinIO'),
        # In-Memory
        ('redis', 'Redis'),
        ('memcached', 'Memcached'),
        ('dragonfly', 'Dragonfly'),
        # Graph
        ('neo4j', 'Neo4j'),
        ('neptune', 'Amazon Neptune'),
        # Time-Series
        ('influxdb', 'InfluxDB'),
        ('timescaledb', 'TimescaleDB'),
        ('clickhouse', 'ClickHouse'),
        # Others
        ('couchdb', 'CouchDB'),

"""
DRF Serializers for Feast Architect
"""
from rest_framework import serializers
from django.contrib.auth.models import User
from .models import (
    FeastRepository, DataSource, Entity,
    AuditLog, LLMChatSession, LLMMessage
)


class UserSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['id', 'username', 'email', 'first_name', 'last_name']


class DataSourceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    category = serializers.CharField(source='category', read_only=True)
    debezium_supported = serializers.BooleanField(source='debezium_supported', read_only=True)
    icon = serializers.SerializerMethodField()
    
    class Meta:
        model = DataSource
        fields = [
            'id', 'name', 'kind', 'category', 'debezium_supported',
            'owned_by', 'access_process', 'connection_string', 'topic',
            'feast_connection_type', 'description', 'tags',
            'pos_x', 'pos_y', 'column_security', 'icon',
            'created_at', 'updated_at'
        ]
    
    def get_icon(self, obj):
        icons = {
            'postgres': '🐘', 'mysql': '🐬', 'sqlserver': '🗃️', 
            'oracle': '🏛️', 'sqlite': '🪶', 'mongodb': '🍃',
            'dynamodb': '⚡', 'cassandra': '🔱', 'couchbase': '🛋️',
            'elasticsearch': '🔍', 'snowflake': '❄️', 'bigquery': '📊',
            'redshift': '🔺', 'databricks': '🧱', 'synapse': '🔷',
            'kafka': '📨', 'kinesis': '💧', 'pulsar': '⭐',
            'eventhubs': '🎯', 's3': '🪣', 'gcs': '☁️',
            'azureblob': '🔵', 'minio': '🪣', 'redis': '🔴',
            'memcached': '🧠', 'dragonfly': '🐉', 'neo4j': '🕸️',
            'neptune': '🌊', 'influxdb': '📈', 'timescaledb': '⏱️',
            'clickhouse': '🖱️', 'couchdb': '🛋️', 'rethinkdb': '🤔',
            'firebase': '🔥', 'supabase': '⚡'
        }
        return icons.get(obj.kind, '🗄️')


class EntitySerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Entity
        fields = [
            'id', 'name', 'join_key', 'description', 'tags',
            'pos_x', 'pos_y', 'created_at', 'updated_at'
        ]


class FeastRepositoryListSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):

        fields = [

            'node_count', 'edge_count', 'created_by_username',
            'created_at', 'updated_at'
        ]

    edge_count = serializers.IntegerField(source='get_edge_count', read_only=True)
    created_by = UserSerializer(read_only=True)
    
    class Meta:
        model = FeastRepository
        fields = [
            'id', 'name', 'location', 'description', 'default_owner',
            'architecture_json', 'settings', 'data_sources', 'entities',
            'node_count', 'edge_count', 'json_hash', 'last_synced_at',
            'created_by', 'created_at', 'updated_at'
        ]

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import CanvasUtils from '../../utils/CanvasUtils.js';

class Canvas {
    constructor(canvasId) {
        this.canvas = document.getElementById(canvasId);
        this.ctx = this.canvas.getContext('2d');
        this.container = this.canvas.parentElement;
        
        this.scale = 1;
        this.offsetX = 50;
        this.offsetY = 50;
        this.isDragging = false;
        this.isPanning = false;
        this.draggedNode = null;
        this.selectedNode = null;
        this.hoveredNode = null;
        this.width = 0;
        this.height = 0;
        
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
        this.resize();
        this._animate();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        this.canvas.addEventListener('mousedown', this._onMouseDown.bind(this));
        this.canvas.addEventListener('mousemove', this._onMouseMove.bind(this));
        this.canvas.addEventListener('mouseup', this._onMouseUp.bind(this));
        this.canvas.addEventListener('wheel', this._onWheel.bind(this));
        this.canvas.addEventListener('dblclick', this._onDoubleClick.bind(this));
        window.addEventListener('resize', this.resize.bind(this));
        
        document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Delete' && this.selectedNode) {
                eventBus.emit('node:delete', { nodeId: this.selectedNode });
            }
        });
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('node:added', () => this.requestRender());
        eventBus.on('node:updated', () => this.requestRender());
        eventBus.on('node:removed', () => {
            if (this.selectedNode && !dataStore.nodes.has(this.selectedNode)) {
                this.selectedNode = null;
            }
            this.requestRender();
        });
        eventBus.on('edge:added', () => this.requestRender());
        eventBus.on('edge:removed', () => this.requestRender());
        eventBus.on('canvas:fit', this.fit.bind(this));
        eventBus.on('canvas:center', ({ nodeId }) => this.centerOnNode(nodeId));
        eventBus.on('canvas:reset', this.resetView.bind(this));
        eventBus.on('canvas:select', ({ nodeId }) => {
            this.selectedNode = nodeId;
            this.requestRender();
        });
    }

    resize() {
        const rect = this.container.getBoundingClientRect();
        const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
        
        this.canvas.width = rect.width * dpr;
        this.canvas.height = rect.height * dpr;
        this.canvas.style.width = `${rect.width}px`;
        this.canvas.style.height = `${rect.height}px`;
        
        this.ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
        this.width = rect.width;
        this.height = rect.height;
        this.requestRender();
    }

    screenToWorld(x, y) {
        return {
            x: (x - this.offsetX) / this.scale,
            y: (y - this.offsetY) / this.scale
        };
    }

    getNodeAt(x, y) {
        const pos = this.screenToWorld(x, y);
        for (const [id, node] of dataStore.nodes) {
            if (pos.x >= node.x && pos.x <= node.x + 200 &&
                pos.y >= node.y && pos.y <= node.y + 100) {
                return id;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    _onMouseDown(e) {
        const rect = this.canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
        const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
        const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
        
... (truncated)

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import CodeGenerationService from '../../services/CodeGenerationService.js';
import FormatUtils from '../../utils/FormatUtils.js';

class CodeEditor {
    constructor() {
        this.panel = document.getElementById('codeEditorPanel');
        this.isOpen = false;
        this.currentFile = 'entities.py';
        this.format = 'python';
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('codeEditorToggleBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.toggle());
        document.getElementById('closeCodeEditor')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.close());
        document.getElementById('codeFormatSelect')?.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            this.format = e.target.value;
            this._render();
        });
        document.getElementById('copyCodeEditor')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._copy());
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('codeeditor:toggle', () => this.toggle());
        eventBus.on('node:updated', () => { if (this.isOpen) this._render(); });
    }

    toggle() {
        this.isOpen = !this.isOpen;
        this.panel.classList.toggle('open', this.isOpen);
        const btn = document.getElementById('codeEditorToggleBtn');
        if (btn) btn.textContent = this.isOpen ? '✕' : '📝';
        if (this.isOpen) this._render();
    }

    close() {
        this.isOpen = false;
        this.panel.classList.remove('open');
        const btn = document.getElementById('codeEditorToggleBtn');
        if (btn) btn.textContent = '📝';
    }

    _render() {
        if (this.format === 'python') this._renderPythonBrowser();
        else if (this.format === 'json') this._renderSingleFile('export.json', 'JSON Export', this._generateJSON());
        else if (this.format === 'yaml') this._renderSingleFile('feature_store.yaml', 'YAML Config', CodeGenerationService.generateYAMLConfig(dataStore.repoSettings));
    }

    _renderPythonBrowser() {
        const files = [

            { name: 'services.py', icon: '🚀', desc: 'Feature services' }

                this._renderPythonBrowser();
                this._renderFileContent();
            });
        });
        this._renderFileContent();
    }

    _renderFileContent() {
        let content = '';
        switch(this.currentFile) {

            case 'data_sources.py': content = CodeGenerationService.generateDataSourcesFile(dataStore.nodes, dataStore.repoSettings); break;
            case 'feature_views.py': content = this._generateFeatureViewsFile(); break;
            case 'services.py': content = this._generateServicesFile(); break;

        document.getElementById('currentFileName').textContent = filename;

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';

class DataFlowModal {
    constructor() {
        this.modal = document.getElementById('dataFlowModal');
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('closeDataFlow')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.close());
        document.getElementById('refreshDataFlow')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._render());
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('dataflow:open', () => this.open());
    }

    open() {
        this._render();
        this.modal.classList.add('active');
    }

    close() {
        this.modal.classList.remove('active');
    }

    _render() {
        const container = document.getElementById('dataFlowStages');
        const stages = [
            { name: 'Source Database', icon: '🗄️', status: 'healthy', details: 'PostgreSQL 14.2\nConnections: 45/100\nReplication: Active' },
            { name: 'Debezium Connector', icon: '⚡', status: 'healthy', details: 'Version: 2.1\nLag: 120ms\nEvents/sec: 1,240' },
            { name: 'Kafka Topic', icon: '📨', status: 'healthy', details: 'Partitions: 12\nReplication: 3\nRetention: 7 days' },
            { name: 'Spark Streaming', icon: '🔥', status: 'warning', details: 'Executors: 4/4\nBatch: 5s\nLatency: 8s ⚠️' },
            { name: 'Postgres Store', icon: '🐘', status: 'healthy', details: 'Size: 2.4TB\nTables: 156\nConnections: 23' }
        ];

        container.innerHTML = stages.map((stage, idx) => `
            <div class="data-flow-stage" data-idx="${idx}">
                <div class="stage-icon">${stage.icon}</div>
                <div class="stage-info">
                    <div class="stage-title">${stage.name}</div>
                    <div class="stage-status">
                        <span class="stage-status-dot status-${stage.status === 'healthy' ? 'green' : stage.status === 'warning' ? 'yellow' : 'red'}"></span>
                        <span style="color: var(--${stage.status === 'healthy' ? 'feast-green' : stage.status === 'warning' ? 'feast-yellow' : 'feast-red'});">
                            ${stage.status === 'healthy' ? 'Healthy' : stage.status === 'warning' ? 'Warning' : 'Error'}
                        </span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="stage-details">${stage.details.replace(/\n/g, '<br>')}</div>
                </div>
            </div>
            ${idx < stages.length - 1 ? '<div class="flow-connector">↓</div>' : ''}
        `).join('');

        container.querySelectorAll('.data-flow-stage').forEach(el => {
            el.addEventListener('click', () => el.classList.toggle('expanded'));
        });
    }
}

export default DataFlowModal;

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import CodeGenerationService from '../../services/CodeGenerationService.js';
import Colors from '../../config/Colors.js';

class DetailPanel {
    constructor() {
        this.panel = document.getElementById('detailPanel');
        this.isOpen = false;
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('closePanelBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.close());
        document.getElementById('editPanelBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (this.currentNodeId) eventBus.emit('node:edit', { nodeId: this.currentNodeId });
        });
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('canvas:select', ({ nodeId }) => this.open(nodeId));
        eventBus.on('node:updated', ({ node }) => {
            if (this.currentNodeId === node.id) this.render(node.id);
        });
        eventBus.on('node:removed', ({ nodeId }) => {
            if (this.currentNodeId === nodeId) this.close();
        });
    }

    open(nodeId) {
        this.currentNodeId = nodeId;
        this.isOpen = true;
        this.panel.classList.add('open');
        this.render(nodeId);
    }

    close() {
        this.currentNodeId = null;
        this.isOpen = false;
        this.panel.classList.remove('open');
        eventBus.emit('panel:closed');
    }

    render(nodeId) {
        const node = dataStore.nodes.get(nodeId);
        if (!node) return;

        const colors = Colors[node.type];
        const icon = node.dbType?.icon || colors.icon;
        
        document.getElementById('panelIcon').textContent = icon;
        document.getElementById('panelType').textContent = colors.label;
        document.getElementById('panelType').style.color = colors.light;
        document.getElementById('panelBadge').style.background = `${colors.bg}20`;
        document.getElementById('panelTitle').textContent = node.name;
        document.getElementById('panelSubtitle').textContent = node.getSubtitle();
        
        const tagsContainer = document.getElementById('panelTags');
        tagsContainer.innerHTML = node.tags?.map(tag => `<span class="tag">#${tag}</span>`).join('') || '';
        
        document.getElementById('panelContent').innerHTML = this._generateContent(node);
    }

    _generateContent(node) {
        let html = '';
        if (node.description) {
            html += this._createSection('Description', `<div class="notes-section"><div class="notes-text">${node.description}</div></div>`);
        }
        html += this._createSection('Details', this._createDetailCard(node));
        if (node.type === 'featureview' && node.features?.length > 0) {
            html += this._createFeaturesSection(node);
        }
        html += this._createLineageSection(node);
        if (node.details?.usedBy?.length > 0) {
            html += this._createUsageSection(node);
        }
        html += this._createCodeSection(node);
        return html;
    }

    _createSection(title, content) {
        return `<div class="panel-section"><div class="section-header"><div class="section-title">${title}</div></div>${content}</div>`;
    }

    _createDetailCard(node) {
        const rows = [];
        switch(node.type) {
            case 'entity':
                rows.push(
                    { label: 'Join Key', value: node.joinKey, highlight: true },
                    { label: 'Used By', value: `${this._getUsedByCount(node.id)} views` }
                );
                break;
            case 'featureview':
                rows.push(
                    { label: 'Type', value: node.subtype, color: this._getSubtypeColor(node.subtype) },
                    { label: 'Entities', value: node.entities?.length || 0 },
                    { label: 'Features', value: node.features?.length || 0 },
                    { label: 'TTL', value: node.details?.ttl || 'Not set' }

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import APIService from '../../services/APIService.js';
import Notification from './Notification.js';

class DjangoAdminPanel {
    constructor() {
        this.panel = document.getElementById('djangoPanel');
        this.isOpen = false;
        this.currentUser = {
            id: window.DJANGO_CONTEXT?.user?.id || 'anonymous',
            name: window.DJANGO_CONTEXT?.user?.name || 'Anonymous',
            initials: this._getInitials(window.DJANGO_CONTEXT?.user?.name),
            role: window.DJANGO_CONTEXT?.user?.isStaff ? 'Admin' : 'User',
            team: 'Data Platform'
        };
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('djangoToggleBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.toggle());
        document.getElementById('closeDjangoPanel')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.close());
        document.getElementById('djangoUserSelector')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._showUserSelector());
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('django:toggle', () => this.toggle());
        eventBus.on('canvas:select', () => { if (this.isOpen) this._renderColumnSecurity(); });
    }

    _getInitials(name) {
        if (!name) return '??';
        return name.split(' ').map(n => n[0]).join('').toUpperCase().substring(0, 2);
    }

    toggle() {
        this.isOpen = !this.isOpen;
        this.panel.classList.toggle('open', this.isOpen);
        if (this.isOpen) this._render();
    }

    close() {
        this.isOpen = false;
        this.panel.classList.remove('open');
    }

    async _render() {
        document.getElementById('djangoCurrentUser').textContent = this.currentUser.name;
        document.getElementById('djangoTeam').textContent = this.currentUser.team;
        document.getElementById('djangoRole').textContent = this.currentUser.role;
        this._renderPermissions();
        this._renderColumnSecurity();
        await this._renderAuditLogs();
    }

    _renderPermissions() {
        const container = document.getElementById('djangoPermissions');
        const datasources = Array.from(dataStore.nodes.values()).filter(n => n.type === 'datasource');
        container.innerHTML = datasources.map(ds => {
            const perm = this._calculatePermission(ds);
            const permClass = { 'owned': 'perm-owned', 'granted': 'perm-granted', 'pending': 'perm-pending', 'denied': 'perm-denied' }[perm];
            const permLabel = { 'owned': '👑 Owned', 'granted': '✅ Granted', 'pending': '⏳ Pending', 'denied': '❌ Denied' }[perm];
            return `<div class="detail-row"><span class="detail-label">${ds.name}</span><span class="permission-badge ${permClass}">${permLabel}</span></div>`;
        }).join('') || '<p style="color: var(--text-muted);">No data sources</p>';
    }

    _calculatePermission(datasource) {
        if (datasource.ownedBy === this.currentUser.team || datasource.ownedBy === this.currentUser.name) return 'owned';
        const hash = datasource.name.split('').reduce((a, b) => a + b.charCodeAt(0), 0);
        return ['granted', 'granted', 'pending', 'denied'][hash % 4];
    }

    _renderColumnSecurity() {
        const container = document.getElementById('djangoColumnSecurity');
        container.innerHTML = '<p style="color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 13px;">Select a data source to view column security</p>';
    }

    async _renderAuditLogs() {
        const container = document.getElementById('djangoAuditLog');
        const mockLogs = [
            { time: '2 min ago', action: 'Viewed', resource: 'User Database', user: this.currentUser.name },
            { time: '15 min ago', action: 'Modified', resource: 'Transaction History', user: this.currentUser.name },
            { time: '1 hour ago', action: 'Created', resource: 'New Feature View', user: this.currentUser.name }
        ];
        container.innerHTML = mockLogs.map(log => `<div class="audit-log-item"><div class="audit-time">${log.time}</div><div><span class="audit-action">${log.action}</span><span style="color: var(--text-muted);"> • </span><span>${log.resource}</span></div><div class="audit-user">${log.user}</div></div>`).join('');
    }

    _showUserSelector() {
        Notification.show('Info', 'User switching not implemented in this version');
    }
}

export default DjangoAdminPanel;

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import EdgeManager from '../../core/EdgeManager.js';
import NodeManager from '../../core/NodeManager.js';
import Colors from '../../config/Colors.js';
import Notification from './Notification.js';

class EdgeManagerPanel {
    constructor() {
        this.panel = document.getElementById('edgeManagerPanel');
        this.isOpen = false;
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('edgeManagerToggleBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.toggle());
        document.getElementById('closeEdgeManager')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.close());
        document.getElementById('addEdgeBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._addEdge());
        document.getElementById('cleanupEdgesBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._cleanupOrphans());
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('edgemanager:toggle', () => this.toggle());
        eventBus.on('edge:added', () => { if (this.isOpen) this._render(); });
        eventBus.on('edge:removed', () => { if (this.isOpen) this._render(); });
    }

    toggle() {
        this.isOpen = !this.isOpen;
        this.panel.classList.toggle('open', this.isOpen);
        if (this.isOpen) { this._render(); this._populateSelects(); }
    }

    close() {
        this.isOpen = false;
        this.panel.classList.remove('open');
    }

    _render() {
        const edgeList = document.getElementById('edgeList');
        const total = dataStore.edges.length;
        const orphaned = EdgeManager.getOrphanedEdges().length;
        const valid = total - orphaned;

        document.getElementById('edgeCountTotal').textContent = total;
        document.getElementById('edgeCountValid').textContent = valid;
        document.getElementById('edgeCountOrphaned').textContent = orphaned;

        if (total === 0) {
            edgeList.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state" style="padding: 40px 20px; text-align: center;"><div style="font-size: 48px; margin-bottom: 16px;">🔗</div><div style="font-weight: 600; margin-bottom: 8px;">No Connections</div><p style="font-size: 13px; color: var(--text-muted);">Create connections between nodes</p></div>`;
            return;
        }

        edgeList.innerHTML = dataStore.edges.map(edge => {
            const fromNode = dataStore.nodes.get(edge.from);
            const toNode = dataStore.nodes.get(edge.to);
            const isValid = fromNode && toNode;
            if (!isValid) return `<div class="edge-item" style="border-color: #ef4444; opacity: 0.7;"><div class="edge-header"><div style="color: #ef4444; font-size: 20px;">⚠️</div><div style="flex: 1;"><div style="font-weight: 500; color: #ef4444;">Orphaned Connection</div><div style="font-size: 12px; color: var(--text-muted);">${!fromNode ? `Missing: ${edge.from}` : ''}${!toNode ? `Missing: ${edge.to}` : ''}</div></div></div><div class="edge-actions"><button class="edge-btn danger" onclick="eventBus.emit('edge:delete', { edgeId: '${edge.id}' })">Delete</button></div></div>`;

            const fromColors = Colors[fromNode.type];
            const toColors = Colors[toNode.type];
            const fromIcon = fromNode.dbType?.icon || fromColors.icon;
            const toIcon = toNode.dbType?.icon || toColors.icon;

            return `<div class="edge-item"><div class="edge-header"><div class="edge-node-icon" style="background: ${fromColors.bg}20; color: ${fromColors.light};">${fromIcon}</div><div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0;"><div style="font-weight: 500; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis;">${fromNode.name}</div><div style="font-size: 11px; color: var(--text-muted);">${fromColors.label}</div></div><span style="margin: 0 8px; color: var(--text-muted);">→</span><div class="edge-node-icon" style="background: ${toColors.bg}20; color: ${toColors.light};">${toIcon}</div><div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0;"><div style="font-weight: 500; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis;">${toNode.name}</div><div style="font-size: 11px; color: var(--text-muted);">${toColors.label}</div></div></div><div class="edge-actions"><button class="edge-btn" onclick="eventBus.emit('canvas:select', { nodeId: '${edge.from}' })">Source</button><button class="edge-btn" onclick="eventBus.emit('canvas:select', { nodeId: '${edge.to}' })">Target</button><button class="edge-btn danger" onclick="eventBus.emit('edge:delete', { edgeId: '${edge.id}' })">Delete</button></div></div>`;
        }).join('');
    }

    _populateSelects() {
        const fromSelect = document.getElementById('edgeFromSelect');
        const toSelect = document.getElementById('edgeToSelect');
        const options = Array.from(dataStore.nodes.values()).map(node => {
            const colors = node.getColors();
            const icon = node.dbType?.icon || colors.icon;
            return `<option value="${node.id}">${icon} ${node.name}</option>`;
        }).join('');
        const defaultOption = '<option value="">Select node...</option>';
        fromSelect.innerHTML = defaultOption + options;
        toSelect.innerHTML = defaultOption + options;
    }

    _addEdge() {
        const fromId = document.getElementById('edgeFromSelect').value;
        const toId = document.getElementById('edgeToSelect').value;
        if (!fromId || !toId) { Notification.warning('Please select both source and target'); return; }
        const edgeId = EdgeManager.create(fromId, toId);
        if (edgeId) {
            Notification.success('Connection created');
            this._render();
            document.getElementById('edgeFromSelect').value = '';
            document.getElementById('edgeToSelect').value = '';
        } else Notification.error('Invalid connection');
    }

    _cleanupOrphans() {
        const count = EdgeManager.cleanupOrphanedEdges();
        Notification.show('Cleanup Complete', `Removed ${count} orphaned connections`);
        this._render();
    }

    _bindEvents() {

        document.getElementById('closeLLMPanel')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.close());
        document.getElementById('llmSendBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._sendMessage());
        this.input?.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') this._sendMessage(); });
        document.getElementById('llmGenerateCode')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._quickAction('generate_code'));
        document.getElementById('llmOptimize')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._quickAction('optimize'));
        document.getElementById('llmLineage')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._quickAction('lineage'));
        document.getElementById('llmValidate')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._quickAction('validate'));
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('llm:toggle', () => this.toggle());
        eventBus.on('canvas:select', () => this._updateContext());
    }

    toggle() {
        this.isOpen = !this.isOpen;
        this.panel.classList.toggle('open', this.isOpen);
        if (this.isOpen) this._updateContext();
    }

    close() {
        this.isOpen = false;
        this.panel.classList.remove('open');
    }

    _updateContext() {
        const stats = dataStore.stats;
        this.contextContent.innerHTML = `
            <div class="llm-context-item"><span>📊</span><span>Architecture: ${stats.datasource + stats.entity + stats.featureview + stats.service} components</span></div>
            <div class="llm-context-item"><span>🔗</span><span>${dataStore.edges.length} connections</span></div>
        `;
    }

    _quickAction(type) {
        const prompts = {
            generate_code: 'Generate Feast code for this architecture',
            optimize: 'Suggest optimizations for my feature views',
            lineage: 'Explain this data lineage',
            validate: 'Validate my entity relationships'
        };
        this._addMessage('user', prompts[type]);
        this._generateResponse(type);
    }

    async _sendMessage() {
        const text = this.input.value.trim();
        if (!text) return;
        this._addMessage('user', text);
        this.input.value = '';

        if (dataStore.repoSettings.id && !this.sessionId) {
            try {
                const api = new APIService();
                const session = await api.createChatSession(dataStore.repoSettings.id, `Chat about ${dataStore.repoSettings.name}`, text);
                this.sessionId = session.id;
                if (session.messages) {
                    const lastMsg = session.messages[session.messages.length - 1];
                    if (lastMsg?.role === 'assistant') { this._addMessage('assistant', lastMsg.content, true); return; }
                }
            } catch (error) { console.log('Backend LLM unavailable, using fallback'); }
        }
        this._generateResponse('default', text);
    }

    _generateResponse(type, customPrompt = null) {
        const loadingId = this._addMessage('assistant', '<div class="spinner"></div> Thinking...', false);
        setTimeout(() => {
            this._removeMessage(loadingId);
            let response = '';
            const selectedNode = this._getSelectedNode();
            switch(type) {
                case 'generate_code': response = this._generateCodeResponse(selectedNode); break;
                case 'optimize': response = this._generateOptimizeResponse(selectedNode); break;
                case 'lineage': response = this._generateLineageResponse(selectedNode); break;
                case 'validate': response = this._generateValidateResponse(); break;
                default: response = this._generateDefaultResponse(customPrompt);
            }
            this._addMessage('assistant', response, true);
        }, 1500);
    }

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';

class MiniMap {
    constructor(canvasId, mainCanvas) {
        this.canvas = document.getElementById(canvasId);
        this.ctx = this.canvas.getContext('2d');
        this.mainCanvas = mainCanvas;
        this.width = 200;
        this.height = 150;
        this.canvas.width = this.width;
        this.canvas.height = this.height;
        this.enabled = true;
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        this.canvas.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            const rect = this.canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
            this._handleClick(e.clientX - rect.left, e.clientY - rect.top);
        });
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('node:added', () => this.render());
        eventBus.on('node:updated', () => this.render());
        eventBus.on('node:removed', () => this.render());
        eventBus.on('viewport:changed', () => this.render());
    }

    _handleClick(x, y) {
        const bounds = dataStore.bounds;
        const scaleX = this.width / bounds.width;
        const scaleY = this.height / bounds.height;
        const scale = Math.min(scaleX, scaleY);
        
        const worldX = (x / scale) - (this.width - bounds.width * scale) / 2 / scale + bounds.minX;
        const worldY = (y / scale) - (this.height - bounds.height * scale) / 2 / scale + bounds.minY;
        
        const targetOffsetX = (this.mainCanvas.width / 2) - worldX * this.mainCanvas.scale;
        const targetOffsetY = (this.mainCanvas.height / 2) - worldY * this.mainCanvas.scale;
        
        eventBus.emit('canvas:panTo', { offsetX: targetOffsetX, offsetY: targetOffsetY });
    }

    render() {
        if (!this.enabled) return;
        
        const bounds = dataStore.bounds;
        const scaleX = this.width / bounds.width;
        const scaleY = this.height / bounds.height;
        const scale = Math.min(scaleX, scaleY) * 0.9;
        
        this.ctx.clearRect(0, 0, this.width, this.height);
        this.ctx.fillStyle = getComputedStyle(document.body).getPropertyValue('--bg-primary').trim() || '#0f172a';
        this.ctx.fillRect(0, 0, this.width, this.height);
        
        this.ctx.save();
        this.ctx.translate(
            (this.width - bounds.width * scale) / 2 - bounds.minX * scale,
            (this.height - bounds.height * scale) / 2 - bounds.minY * scale
        );
        this.ctx.scale(scale, scale);
        
        this.ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)';
        this.ctx.lineWidth = 2 / scale;
        
        dataStore.edges.forEach(edge => {
            const from = dataStore.nodes.get(edge.from);
            const to = dataStore.nodes.get(edge.to);
            if (!from || !to) return;
            this.ctx.beginPath();
            this.ctx.moveTo(from.x + 100, from.y + 50);
            this.ctx.lineTo(to.x + 100, to.y + 50);
            this.ctx.stroke();
        });
        
        dataStore.nodes.forEach(node => {
            const colors = node.getColors();
            this.ctx.fillStyle = colors.bg;
            this.ctx.fillRect(node.x, node.y, 200, 100);
        });
        
        this.ctx.restore();
        
        const vpX = (-this.mainCanvas.offsetX / this.mainCanvas.scale - bounds.minX) * scale + 
                   (this.width - bounds.width * scale) / 2;
        const vpY = (-this.mainCanvas.offsetY / this.mainCanvas.scale - bounds.minY) * scale + 
                   (this.height - bounds.height * scale) / 2;
        const vpW = (this.mainCanvas.width / this.mainCanvas.scale) * scale;
        const vpH = (this.mainCanvas.height / this.mainCanvas.scale) * scale;
        
        this.ctx.strokeStyle = '#f97316';
        this.ctx.lineWidth = 2;
        this.ctx.strokeRect(vpX, vpY, vpW, vpH);
    }

    toggle() {
        this.enabled = !this.enabled;
... (truncated)

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import NodeManager from '../../core/NodeManager.js';
import EdgeManager from '../../core/EdgeManager.js';
import DatabaseTypes from '../../config/DatabaseTypes.js';
import Notification from './Notification.js';

class NodeModal {
    constructor() {
        this.modal = document.getElementById('componentModal');
        this.titleEl = document.getElementById('modalTitle');
        this.bodyEl = document.getElementById('modalBody');
        this.deleteBtn = document.getElementById('deleteBtn');
        this.currentType = null;
        this.currentNodeId = null;
        this.tempFeatures = [];
        this.tempTags = [];
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        this.modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (e.target === this.modal) this.close(); });
        this.deleteBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (this.currentNodeId && confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this node?')) {
                dataStore.removeNode(this.currentNodeId);
                this.close();
                Notification.show('Deleted', 'Node removed');
            }
        });
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('modal:open', ({ type, mode, nodeId }) => {
            mode === 'edit' && nodeId ? this.openEdit(type, nodeId) : this.openCreate(type);
        });
        eventBus.on('node:edit', ({ nodeId }) => {
            const node = dataStore.nodes.get(nodeId);
            if (node) this.openEdit(node.type, nodeId);
        });
    }

    openCreate(type) {
        this.currentType = type;
        this.currentNodeId = null;
        this.tempFeatures = [];
        this.tempTags = [];
        this.deleteBtn.style.display = 'none';
        this._render(type);
        this.modal.classList.add('active');
    }

    openEdit(type, nodeId) {
        const node = dataStore.nodes.get(nodeId);
        if (!node) return;
        this.currentType = type;
        this.currentNodeId = nodeId;
        this.tempFeatures = node.features ? [...node.features] : [];
        this.tempTags = node.tags ? [...node.tags] : [];
        this.deleteBtn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
        this._render(type, node);
        this.modal.classList.add('active');
    }

    _render(type, existingNode = null) {
        const titles = {
            datasource: existingNode ? 'Edit Data Source' : 'Add Data Source',
            entity: existingNode ? 'Edit Entity' : 'Add Entity',
            featureview: existingNode ? 'Edit Feature View' : 'Add Feature View',
            service: existingNode ? 'Edit Feature Service' : 'Add Feature Service'
        };
        this.titleEl.textContent = titles[type];
        
        let html = this._createCommonFields(existingNode);
        switch(type) {
            case 'datasource': html += this._createDataSourceFields(existingNode); break;
            case 'entity': html += this._createEntityFields(existingNode); break;
            case 'featureview': html += this._createFeatureViewFields(existingNode); break;
            case 'service': html += this._createServiceFields(existingNode); break;
        }
        html += this._createTagsSection() + this._createDescriptionFields(existingNode) + this._createActions();
        this.bodyEl.innerHTML = html;
        this._attachDynamicListeners();
    }

    _createCommonFields(node) {
        return `<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Name *</label><input type="text" class="form-input" id="inputName" value="${node?.name || ''}" placeholder="e.g., User Demographics"></div>`;
    }

    _createDataSourceFields(node) {
        const dbOptions = Object.entries(DatabaseTypes).map(([key, db]) => {
            const selected = node?.kind === key ? 'selected' : '';
            return `<option value="${key}" ${selected}>${db.icon} ${db.name}</option>`;
        }).join('');
        return `
            <div class="form-row">
                <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Source Type</label><select class="form-select" id="inputKind">${dbOptions}</select></div>
                <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Connection</label><input type="text" class="form-input" id="inputConnection" value="${node?.details?.connection || ''}" placeholder="host:port/db"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Owned By</label><input type="text" class="form-input" id="inputOwnedBy" value="${node?.ownedBy || dataStore.repoSettings.defaultOwner}"></div>

class Notification {
    constructor() {
        this.container = document.getElementById('notification');
        this.titleEl = document.getElementById('notifTitle');
        this.textEl = document.getElementById('notifText');
        this.hideTimeout = null;
    }

    show(title, text, duration = 3000) {
        this.titleEl.textContent = title;
        this.textEl.textContent = text;
        this.container.classList.add('show');
        clearTimeout(this.hideTimeout);
        this.hideTimeout = setTimeout(() => this.hide(), duration);
    }

    hide() {
        this.container.classList.remove('show');
    }

    success(text, duration) {
        this.show('Success', text, duration);
    }

    error(text, duration = 5000) {
        this.show('Error', text, duration);
    }

    warning(text, duration) {
        this.show('Warning', text, duration);
    }
}

export default new Notification();

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import Colors from '../../config/Colors.js';

class SearchDropdown {
    constructor() {
        this.input = document.getElementById('searchInput');
        this.dropdown = document.getElementById('searchDropdown');
        this.content = document.getElementById('searchDropdownContent');
        this.settings = { descriptions: true, tags: true, usedBy: true, access: true };
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        this.input.addEventListener('input', (e) => this._handleInput(e));
        this.input.addEventListener('focus', () => { if (this.input.value.trim()) this._show(); });
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (!e.target.closest('.search-box')) this._hide();
        });
        this.input.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Escape') { this._hide(); this.input.blur(); }
        });
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('search:focus', () => this.input.focus());
    }

    _handleInput(e) {
        const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
        if (!query) { this._hide(); return; }
        const results = this._performSearch(query);
        this._renderResults(results, query);
        this._show();
    }

    _performSearch(query) {
        const results = { featureview: [], feature: [], entity: [], service: [], datasource: [] };
        dataStore.nodes.forEach((node, id) => {
            if (node.name.toLowerCase().includes(query)) {
                this._addResult(results, node, id, 'name', node.name);
            }
            if (this.settings.descriptions && node.description?.toLowerCase().includes(query)) {
                this._addResult(results, node, id, 'description', node.description);
            }
            if (this.settings.tags && node.tags) {
                node.tags.forEach(tag => {
                    if (tag.toLowerCase().includes(query)) this._addResult(results, node, id, 'tag', tag);
                });
            }
            if (node.type === 'featureview' && node.features) {
                node.features.forEach(feature => {
                    const featureName = typeof feature === 'string' ? feature : feature.name;
                    if (featureName.toLowerCase().includes(query)) {
                        results.feature.push({
                            type: 'feature', nodeType: 'feature', id, name: featureName,
                            parentName: node.name, matchType: 'feature',
                            dataType: typeof feature === 'string' ? 'Unknown' : feature.type
                        });
                    }
                });
            }
            if (this.settings.access && node.type === 'datasource' && node.accessProcess?.toLowerCase().includes(query)) {
                this._addResult(results, node, id, 'access', node.accessProcess);
            }
        });
        Object.keys(results).forEach(key => results[key] = results[key].slice(0, 5));
        return results;
    }

    _addResult(results, node, id, matchType, matchText) {
        const result = { type: 'node', nodeType: node.type, id, name: node.name, matchType, matchText };
        if (results[node.type] && !results[node.type].find(r => r.id === id && r.matchType === matchType)) {
            results[node.type].push(result);
        }
    }

    _renderResults(grouped, query) {
        const categories = [
            { key: 'featureview', label: 'Feature Views', icon: '📊', color: '#10b981' },
            { key: 'feature', label: 'Features', icon: '⚡', color: '#06b6d4' },
            { key: 'entity', label: 'Entities', icon: '👤', color: '#8b5cf6' },
            { key: 'service', label: 'Services', icon: '🚀', color: '#f97316' },
            { key: 'datasource', label: 'Data Sources', icon: '🗄️', color: '#3b82f6' }
        ];

        let html = '';
        categories.forEach(cat => {
            const items = grouped[cat.key];
            if (items && items.length > 0) {
                html += `<div class="search-category">
                    <div class="search-category-header"><span class="search-category-icon">${cat.icon}</span><span>${cat.label}</span></div>
                    ${items.map(item => this._renderResultItem(item, cat, query)).join('')}
                </div>`;
            }
        });
        if (html === '') html = '<div class="search-no-results">No results found</div>';
        this.content.innerHTML = html;

... (truncated)

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import APIService from '../../services/APIService.js';
import Notification from './Notification.js';

class SettingsModal {
    constructor() {
        this.modal = document.getElementById('settingsModal');
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('closeSettings')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.close());
        document.getElementById('saveSettings')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.save());
        ['Descriptions', 'Tags', 'UsedBy', 'Access'].forEach(setting => {
            const btn = document.getElementById(`toggle${setting}`);
            btn?.addEventListener('click', () => btn.classList.toggle('active'));
        });
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('settings:open', () => this.open());
    }

    open() {
        const settings = dataStore.repoSettings;
        document.getElementById('settingsRepoName').value = settings.name;
        document.getElementById('settingsRepoLocation').value = settings.location;
        document.getElementById('settingsRepoDescription').value = settings.description || '';
        document.getElementById('settingsDefaultOwner').value = settings.defaultOwner;
        this.modal.classList.add('active');
    }

    async save() {
        const newSettings = {
            name: document.getElementById('settingsRepoName').value || 'feature_repo',
            location: document.getElementById('settingsRepoLocation').value || '/opt/feast',
            defaultOwner: document.getElementById('settingsDefaultOwner').value || 'Data Platform Team',
            description: document.getElementById('settingsRepoDescription').value || ''
        };

        dataStore.repoSettings = { ...dataStore.repoSettings, ...newSettings };
        
        if (dataStore.repoSettings.id) {
            try {
                const api = new APIService();
                await api.patchRepository(dataStore.repoSettings.id, {
                    name: newSettings.name, location: newSettings.location,
                    default_owner: newSettings.defaultOwner, description: newSettings.description
                });
                Notification.show('Settings Saved', 'Repository updated on server');
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Failed to save settings:', error);
                Notification.show('Warning', 'Saved locally but not synced to server');
            }
        } else {
            Notification.show('Settings Saved', 'Repository configuration updated');
        }
        eventBus.emit('repo:updated', { settings: dataStore.repoSettings });
        this.close();
    }

    close() {
        this.modal.classList.remove('active');
    }
}

export default SettingsModal;

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import Colors from '../../config/Colors.js';

class StatsModal {
    constructor() {
        this.modal = document.getElementById('statsModal');
        this._bindEvents();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('closeStats')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.close());
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('stats:open', () => this.open());
    }

    open() {
        this._renderStats();
        this._renderFileTree();
        this.modal.classList.add('active');
    }

    _renderStats() {
        const stats = {
            datasource: { count: 0, items: [], color: '#3b82f6', icon: '🗄️' },
            entity: { count: 0, items: [], color: '#8b5cf6', icon: '👤' },
            featureview: { count: 0, items: [], color: '#10b981', icon: '📊' },
            service: { count: 0, items: [], color: '#f97316', icon: '🚀' }
        };

        dataStore.nodes.forEach((node, id) => {
            if (stats[node.type]) {
                stats[node.type].count++;
                stats[node.type].items.push(node.name);
            }
        });

        const grid = document.getElementById('statsGrid');
        grid.innerHTML = Object.entries(stats).map(([type, data]) => `
            <div class="stat-detail-card">
                <div class="stat-detail-header">
                    <div class="stat-detail-icon" style="background: ${data.color}20; color: ${data.color};">${data.icon}</div>
                    <div><div class="stat-detail-title">${Colors[type].label}s</div><div class="stat-detail-value">${data.count}</div></div>
                </div>
                <div class="stat-detail-list">
                    ${data.items.map(item => `<div class="stat-detail-item"><span>${item}</span><span style="color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 11px;">${type}</span></div>`).join('')}
                </div>
            </div>
        `).join('');
    }

    _renderFileTree() {
        const sources = Array.from(dataStore.nodes.values()).filter(n => n.type === 'datasource');
        const tree = document.getElementById('fileTree');
        tree.innerHTML = `
            <div class="file-tree-item dir">${dataStore.repoSettings.name}/</div>
            <div class="file-tree-item dir" style="padding-left: 40px;">data/</div>
            <div class="file-tree-item" style="padding-left: 60px;">registry.db</div>
            ${sources.map(n => `<div class="file-tree-item" style="padding-left: 60px;">${n.name.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '_')}.parquet</div>`).join('')}
            <div class="file-tree-item" style="padding-left: 40px;">entities.py</div>
            <div class="file-tree-item" style="padding-left: 40px;">data_sources.py</div>
            <div class="file-tree-item" style="padding-left: 40px;">feature_views.py</div>
            <div class="file-tree-item" style="padding-left: 40px;">services.py</div>
            <div class="file-tree-item" style="padding-left: 40px;">feature_store.yaml</div>
        `;
    }

    close() {
        this.modal.classList.remove('active');
    }
}

export default StatsModal;

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import Colors from '../../config/Colors.js';

class Tooltip {
    constructor() {
        this.element = document.getElementById('tooltip');
        this.visible = false;
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        eventBus.on('node:hover', ({ nodeId, x, y }) => this.show(nodeId, x, y));
        eventBus.on('node:hover:end', () => this.hide());
    }

    show(nodeId, x, y) {
        const node = dataStore.nodes.get(nodeId);
        if (!node) return;

        const colors = node.getColors();
        const icon = node.dbType?.icon || colors.icon;
        let subtitle = colors.label;
        if (node.subtype) subtitle += ` • ${node.subtype}`;
        if (node.dbType) subtitle += ` • ${node.dbType.name}`;

        const tagsHtml = node.tags?.slice(0, 3).map(tag => `<span class="tooltip-tag">#${tag}</span>`).join('') || '';
        
        let featuresHtml = '';
        if (node.features?.length > 0) {
            const featureTags = node.features.slice(0, 5).map(f => `<span class="tooltip-feature-tag">${f.name}</span>`).join('');
            const more = node.features.length > 5 ? `<span style="color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 11px;">+${node.features.length - 5} more</span>` : '';
            featuresHtml = `<div id="tooltipFeatures"><div id="tooltipFeatureList">${featureTags}${more}</div></div>`;
        }

        const descHtml = node.description ? `<div id="tooltipDescription"><div id="tooltipDescText">${node.description.substring(0, 100)}${node.description.length > 100 ? '...' : ''}</div></div>` : '';

        this.element.innerHTML = `
            <div id="tooltipIcon">${icon}</div>
            <div id="tooltipTitle">${node.name}</div>
            <div id="tooltipSubtitle">${subtitle}</div>
            <div id="tooltipTags">${tagsHtml}</div>
            ${featuresHtml}
            ${descHtml}
        `;

        const tooltipWidth = 320;
        const tooltipHeight = 200;
        let left = x + 20;
        let top = y + 20;
        
        if (left + tooltipWidth > window.innerWidth) left = x - tooltipWidth - 20;
        if (top + tooltipHeight > window.innerHeight) top = y - tooltipHeight - 20;

        this.element.style.left = `${Math.max(10, left)}px`;
        this.element.style.top = `${Math.max(10, top)}px`;
        this.element.style.display = 'block';
        this.visible = true;
    }

    hide() {
        this.element.style.display = 'none';
        this.visible = false;
    }
}

export default Tooltip;

import { eventBus } from './EventBus.js';
import APIService from '../services/APIService.js';

class DataStore {
    constructor() {
        this.nodes = new Map();
        this.edges = [];
        this.repoSettings = {
            name: 'enterprise_feature_store',
            location: '/opt/feast/feature_repo',
            defaultOwner: 'Data Platform Team',
            id: null,
            description: ''
        };
        this.counters = { datasource: 0, entity: 0, featureview: 0, service: 0 };
        this.api = new APIService();
        this._setupEventListeners();
    }

    _setupEventListeners() {
        let debounceTimer;
        eventBus.on('state:changed', () => {
            clearTimeout(debounceTimer);
            debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => this._persist(), 5000);
        });
    }

    generateId(type) {
        if (!this.counters[type]) this.counters[type] = 0;
        return `${type}_${++this.counters[type]}`;
    }

    setNode(node) {
        const isNew = !this.nodes.has(node.id);
        this.nodes.set(node.id, node);
        eventBus.emit(isNew ? 'node:added' : 'node:updated', { node });
        eventBus.emit('state:changed', { type: 'node', action: isNew ? 'add' : 'update' });
        return node.id;
    }

    removeNode(id) {
        const node = this.nodes.get(id);
        if (!node) return false;

        this.edges = this.edges.filter(edge => {
            const isConnected = edge.from === id || edge.to === id;
            if (isConnected) eventBus.emit('edge:removed', { edge });
            return !isConnected;
        });

        this.nodes.forEach(n => {
            n.inputs = n.inputs.filter(i => i !== id);
            n.outputs = n.outputs.filter(o => o !== id);
        });

        this.nodes.delete(id);
        eventBus.emit('node:removed', { nodeId: id, node });
        eventBus.emit('state:changed', { type: 'node', action: 'remove' });
        return true;
    }

    addEdge(fromId, toId) {
        const fromNode = this.nodes.get(fromId);
        const toNode = this.nodes.get(toId);
        
        if (!fromNode || !toNode) return null;
        if (fromId === toId) return null;
        
        const validConnections = {
            'entity': ['featureview'],
            'datasource': ['featureview'],
            'featureview': ['service'],
            'service': ['service']
        };
        
        if (!validConnections[fromNode.type]?.includes(toNode.type)) {
            console.warn(`Invalid connection: ${fromNode.type} → ${toNode.type}`);
            return null;
        }

        const exists = this.edges.some(e => e.from === fromId && e.to === toId);
        if (exists) return null;

        const edge = { id: `${fromId}->${toId}`, from: fromId, to: toId, animated: false };
        this.edges.push(edge);
        
        fromNode.outputs.push(toId);
        toNode.inputs.push(fromId);
        
        eventBus.emit('edge:added', { edge });
        eventBus.emit('state:changed', { type: 'edge', action: 'add' });
        return edge.id;
    }

    removeEdge(edgeId) {
        const index = this.edges.findIndex(e => e.id === edgeId);
        if (index === -1) return false;

        const edge = this.edges[index];
        const fromNode = this.nodes.get(edge.from);
... (truncated)

import dataStore from './DataStore.js';
import NodeManager from './NodeManager.js';
import { eventBus } from './EventBus.js';

class EdgeManager {
    create(fromId, toId) {
        const fromNode = dataStore.nodes.get(fromId);
        const toNode = dataStore.nodes.get(toId);

        if (!fromNode || !toNode) {
            console.warn('Cannot create edge: missing node');
            return null;
        }

        if (!NodeManager.isValidConnection(fromNode.type, toNode.type)) {
            console.warn(`Invalid connection: ${fromNode.type} → ${toNode.type}`);
            return null;
        }

        const edgeId = dataStore.addEdge(fromId, toId);
        
        if (edgeId) {
            if (toNode.type === 'featureview' && fromNode.type === 'entity') {
                if (!toNode.entities.includes(fromId)) toNode.entities.push(fromId);
            }
            if (toNode.type === 'service' && fromNode.type === 'featureview') {
                if (!toNode.features.includes(fromId)) toNode.features.push(fromId);
            }
        }

        return edgeId;
    }

    remove(edgeId) {
        const edge = dataStore.edges.find(e => e.id === edgeId);
        if (!edge) return;

        dataStore.removeEdge(edgeId);

        const toNode = dataStore.nodes.get(edge.to);
        if (toNode) {
            if (toNode.type === 'featureview') {
                toNode.entities = toNode.entities.filter(id => id !== edge.from);
            }
            if (toNode.type === 'service') {
                toNode.features = toNode.features.filter(id => id !== edge.from);
            }
        }
    }

    getNodeEdges(nodeId) {
        return {
            inputs: dataStore.edges.filter(e => e.to === nodeId),
            outputs: dataStore.edges.filter(e => e.from === nodeId)
        };
    }

    getAncestors(nodeId, maxDepth = 10) {
        const ancestors = new Set();
        const queue = [[nodeId, 0]];
        
        while (queue.length > 0) {
            const [currentId, depth] = queue.shift();
            if (depth >= maxDepth) continue;
            
            const edges = dataStore.edges.filter(e => e.to === currentId);
            edges.forEach(edge => {
                if (!ancestors.has(edge.from)) {
                    ancestors.add(edge.from);
                    queue.push([edge.from, depth + 1]);
                }
            });
        }
        return Array.from(ancestors);
    }

    getDescendants(nodeId, maxDepth = 10) {
        const descendants = new Set();
        const queue = [[nodeId, 0]];
        
        while (queue.length > 0) {
            const [currentId, depth] = queue.shift();
            if (depth >= maxDepth) continue;
            
            const edges = dataStore.edges.filter(e => e.from === currentId);
            edges.forEach(edge => {
                if (!descendants.has(edge.to)) {
                    descendants.add(edge.to);
                    queue.push([edge.to, depth + 1]);
                }
            });
        }
        return Array.from(descendants);
    }

    findPath(fromId, toId) {
        const visited = new Set();
        const queue = [[fromId]];
        
        while (queue.length > 0) {

File: ./FeastArchitect/static/FeastArchitect/Core/EventBus.js
============================================================
/**
 * EventBus - Pub/Sub pattern for decoupled component communication
 */
class EventBus {
    constructor() {
        this.events = new Map();
    }

    on(event, callback) {
        if (!this.events.has(event)) {
            this.events.set(event, new Set());
        }
        this.events.get(event).add(callback);
        return () => this.events.get(event).delete(callback);
    }

    emit(event, data) {
        if (this.events.has(event)) {
            this.events.get(event).forEach(callback => {
                try {
                    callback(data);
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error(`Error in event handler for ${event}:`, error);
                }
            });
        }
    }

    off(event) {
        this.events.delete(event);
    }
}

export const eventBus = new EventBus();
export default EventBus;

File: ./FeastArchitect/static/FeastArchitect/Core/NodeManager.js

import DataSource from '../models/DataSource.js';
import Entity from '../models/Entity.js';
import FeatureView from '../models/FeatureView.js';
import FeatureService from '../models/FeatureService.js';
import dataStore from './DataStore.js';

class NodeManager {
    create(type, config) {
        const id = dataStore.generateId(type);
        const baseConfig = { ...config, id, type };

        switch(type) {
            case 'datasource': return new DataSource(baseConfig);
            case 'entity': return new Entity(baseConfig);
            case 'featureview': return new FeatureView(baseConfig);
            case 'service': return new FeatureService(baseConfig);
            default: throw new Error(`Unknown node type: ${type}`);
        }
    }

    isValidConnection(fromType, toType) {
        const validConnections = {
            'entity': ['featureview'],
            'datasource': ['featureview'],
            'featureview': ['service'],
            'service': ['service']
        };
        return validConnections[fromType]?.includes(toType) || false;
    }

    getByType(type) {
        return Array.from(dataStore.nodes.values()).filter(n => n.type === type);
    }

    findByTag(tag) {
        return Array.from(dataStore.nodes.values()).filter(n => 
            n.tags?.includes(tag.toLowerCase())
        );
    }

    calculateBounds() {
        const nodes = Array.from(dataStore.nodes.values());
        if (nodes.length === 0) {
            return { minX: 0, minY: 0, maxX: 1000, maxY: 800, centerX: 500, centerY: 400 };
        }

        const xs = nodes.map(n => n.x);
        const ys = nodes.map(n => n.y);
        
        return {
            minX: Math.min(...xs),
            minY: Math.min(...ys),
            maxX: Math.max(...xs) + 200,
            maxY: Math.max(...ys) + 100,
            centerX: (Math.min(...xs) + Math.max(...xs) + 200) / 2,
            centerY: (Math.min(...ys) + Math.max(...ys) + 100) / 2
        };
    }

    calculateAutoLayout() {
        const columns = { datasource: [], entity: [], featureview: [], service: [] };
        dataStore.nodes.forEach((node, id) => {
            if (columns[node.type]) columns[node.type].push({ id, node });
        });

        const colWidth = 280;
        const rowHeight = 140;
        const startX = 120;
        const startY = 120;
        const positions = [];

        let colIndex = 0;
        ['datasource', 'entity', 'featureview', 'service'].forEach(type => {
            const colNodes = columns[type];
            if (colNodes.length === 0) return;

            colNodes.sort((a, b) => 
                (b.node.inputs.length + b.node.outputs.length) - 
                (a.node.inputs.length + a.node.outputs.length)
            );

            const colX = startX + colIndex * colWidth;
            const totalHeight = colNodes.length * rowHeight;
            const colY = Math.max(startY, 400 - totalHeight / 2);

            colNodes.forEach(({ id, node }, idx) => {
                positions.push({ id, x: colX, y: colY + idx * rowHeight, originalX: node.x, originalY: node.y });
            });
            colIndex++;
        });

        return positions;
    }
}

export default new NodeManager();

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';

class FloatingActions {
    constructor() {
        this.menuOpen = false;
        this._bindEvents();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('fabMain')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._toggleMenu());
        document.getElementById('fabSource')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._addNode('datasource'));
        document.getElementById('fabEntity')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._addNode('entity'));
        document.getElementById('fabView')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._addNode('featureview'));
        document.getElementById('fabService')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._addNode('service'));
        document.getElementById('zoomInBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('canvas:zoom', { delta: 1.2 }));
        document.getElementById('zoomOutBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('canvas:zoom', { delta: 0.8 }));
        document.getElementById('fitBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('canvas:fit'));
        document.getElementById('resetViewBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('canvas:reset'));
        document.getElementById('autoLayoutBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('layout:auto'));
        document.getElementById('pushRepoBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('repo:push'));
        document.getElementById('refreshRepoBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('repo:refresh'));
    }

    _toggleMenu() {
        this.menuOpen = !this.menuOpen;
        const buttons = ['fabSource', 'fabEntity', 'fabView', 'fabService'];
        buttons.forEach((id, idx) => {
            setTimeout(() => {
                const btn = document.getElementById(id);
                if (btn) btn.style.display = this.menuOpen ? 'flex' : 'none';
            }, idx * 50);
        });
    }

    _addNode(type) {
        this._toggleMenu();
        eventBus.emit('modal:open', { type, mode: 'create' });
    }
}

export default FloatingActions;

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';

class Sidebar {
    constructor() {
        this.layers = { datasource: true, entity: true, featureview: true, service: true };
        this._bindEvents();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('toggleSources')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._toggle('datasource'));
        document.getElementById('toggleEntities')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._toggle('entity'));
        document.getElementById('toggleViews')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._toggle('featureview'));
        document.getElementById('toggleServices')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._toggle('service'));
    }

    _toggle(type) {
        this.layers[type] = !this.layers[type];
        const btn = document.getElementById(`toggle${type.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + type.slice(1)}s`);
        const eyeIcon = btn?.querySelector('.eye-icon');
        if (this.layers[type]) {
            btn?.classList.remove('hidden-layer');
            if (eyeIcon) eyeIcon.textContent = '👁';
        } else {
            btn?.classList.add('hidden-layer');
            if (eyeIcon) eyeIcon.textContent = '🚫';
        }
        eventBus.emit('layer:toggle', { type, visible: this.layers[type] });
    }

    isVisible(type) {
        return this.layers[type];
    }
}

export default Sidebar;

import { eventBus } from '../../core/EventBus.js';
import dataStore from '../../core/DataStore.js';
import ExportImportService from '../../services/ExportImportService.js';
import Notification from '../components/Notification.js';

class Toolbar {
    constructor() {
        this._bindEvents();
    }

    _bindEvents() {
        document.getElementById('themeToggleBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._toggleTheme());
        document.getElementById('settingsBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('settings:open'));
        document.getElementById('exportBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._export());
        document.getElementById('importBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._import());
        document.getElementById('resetBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this._reset());
        document.getElementById('guideBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('guide:open'));
        document.getElementById('statsBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => eventBus.emit('stats:open'));
    }

    _toggleTheme() {
        const html = document.documentElement;
        const current = html.getAttribute('data-theme') || 'dark';
        const next = current === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark';
        html.setAttribute('data-theme', next);
        document.getElementById('themeIcon').textContent = next === 'dark' ? '☀️' : '🌙';
        Notification.show('Theme Changed', `Switched to ${next} mode`);
        eventBus.emit('theme:changed', { theme: next });
    }

    async _export() {
        try {
            const service = new ExportImportService();
            await service.export(dataStore);
            Notification.success('Architecture exported');
        } catch (error) {
            Notification.error('Export failed: ' + error.message);
        }
    }

    _import() {
        const service = new ExportImportService();
        service.import((data) => {
            dataStore.fromJSON(data);
            eventBus.emit('canvas:fit');
            Notification.success('Architecture imported');
        });
    }

    _reset() {
        if (!confirm('Reset to example data? All unsaved changes will be lost.')) return;
        dataStore.nodes.clear();
        dataStore.edges = [];
        import('../../utils/ExampleData.js').then(module => {
            module.loadComplexExample(dataStore);
            eventBus.emit('canvas:fit');
            Notification.show('Reset', 'Diagram reset to example data');
        });
    }
}

export default Toolbar;
